# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="ab011-102">.NET Framework 中的过时成员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ab011-103">本文中的表列出了 .NET Framework 4.5 和更高版本中由程序集组织的已过时的类型成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ab011-104">使用以下链接可查看每个程序集中过时的成员和建议的备选项的列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ab011-105">本文未列出过时类型的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ab011-106">有关过时类型的列表，请参阅 [过时类型](obsolete-types.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

<a name="SystemMembers"></a>

## <a name="obsolete-members-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="ab011-140">系统程序集中的过时成员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-140">Obsolete Members in System Assemblies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ab011-141">下表列出了系统程序集中的过时成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-141">The following tables list the obsolete members in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ab011-142">这些程序集用于面向 .NET Framework 的通用\-应用程序开发。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-142">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

<a name="IEHost"></a>

### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="ab011-1147">程序集：IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-1147">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ab011-1148">IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe 程序集已从 .NET Framework 中删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-1148">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ab011-1149">其所有类型和成员已过时，且在 .NET Framework 4.5 中不受支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-1149">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported in the .NET Framework 4.5.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ab011-1150">这些程序集过去用于承载 Windows 窗体控件和在 Internet Explorer 中运行可执行文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-1150">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ab011-1151">该技术的替代项包括 ClickOnce、XAML 浏览器应用程序 (XBAP) 和 Microsoft Silverlight。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ab011-1151">Alternatives to this technology include ClickOnce, XAML Browser Applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
